<text>SO happy that I found this place during quarantine. I saw a photo of their cheong fun on instagram and was excited that this place was located near me. I've been here countless times since prices are cheap and affordable. They're fast and the food tastes great. Should note that they take cash only, but I think they accept venmo as well. I've tried their cheong fun with shrimp, beef, egg and corn, and liver. All of them have been great and I love this style of cheong fun, where the toppings are on top, rather than inside. Cash only to be prepped and brought over!

I haven't had Hong Kong cafe grub food for days and this simply just hits the spot!

Their rice noodle rolls are delicious and so fresh with complimenting squishable bottled sweet soy sauce to go squirt all over it!  They have many fillings to choose from and my favorite was the shrimp and beef!

Hong Kong iced milk tea for the refreshing win!
